<h2 data-start="113" data-end="155">🏗️ <strong data-start="120" data-end="155">1. Jenkins Installation &amp; Setup</strong></h2>
<h3 data-start="157" data-end="190">🔹 <strong data-start="164" data-end="190">Lab 1: Install Jenkins</strong></h3>
<ul data-start="191" data-end="293">
<li data-start="191" data-end="293">
<p data-start="193" data-end="212">Install Jenkins on:</p>
<ul data-start="215" data-end="293">
<li data-start="215" data-end="247">
<p data-start="217" data-end="247">Docker (<code data-start="225" data-end="246">jenkins/jenkins:lts</code>)</p>
</li>
<li data-start="250" data-end="270">
<p data-start="252" data-end="270">Ubuntu (apt-based)</p>
</li>
<li data-start="273" data-end="293">
<p data-start="275" data-end="293">Windows (optional)</p>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
<p data-start="295" data-end="353">✅ Verify by accessing Jenkins Web UI (<code data-start="333" data-end="351">http://&lt;IP&gt;:8080</code>).</p>
<hr data-start="355" data-end="358">
<h3 data-start="360" data-end="395">🔹 <strong data-start="367" data-end="395">Lab 2: Configure Jenkins</strong></h3>
<ul data-start="396" data-end="595">
<li data-start="396" data-end="418">
<p data-start="398" data-end="418">Create an admin user</p>
</li>
<li data-start="419" data-end="444">
<p data-start="421" data-end="444">Install default plugins</p>
</li>
<li data-start="445" data-end="595">
<p data-start="447" data-end="476">Install additional plugins:</p>
<ul data-start="479" data-end="595">
<li data-start="479" data-end="595">
<p data-start="481" data-end="595"><strong data-start="481" data-end="488">Git</strong>, <strong data-start="490" data-end="502">Pipeline</strong>, <strong data-start="504" data-end="518">Blue Ocean</strong>, <strong data-start="520" data-end="530">Docker</strong>, <strong data-start="532" data-end="554">GitHub Integration</strong>, <strong data-start="556" data-end="563">SSH</strong>, <strong data-start="565" data-end="575">NodeJS</strong>, <strong data-start="577" data-end="595">Kubernetes CLI</strong></p>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
<p data-start="597" data-end="647">✅ Verify plugins via "Manage Jenkins" &gt; "Plugins".</p>
<hr data-start="649" data-end="652">
<h2 data-start="654" data-end="693">🔨 <strong data-start="660" data-end="693">2. Jenkins Freestyle Projects</strong></h2>
<h3 data-start="695" data-end="729">🔹 <strong data-start="702" data-end="729">Lab 3: Simple Build Job</strong></h3>
<ul data-start="730" data-end="837">
<li data-start="730" data-end="837">
<p data-start="732" data-end="759">Create a <strong data-start="741" data-end="758">Freestyle Job</strong>:</p>
<ul data-start="762" data-end="837">
<li data-start="762" data-end="790">
<p data-start="764" data-end="790">Git checkout a sample repo</p>
</li>
<li data-start="793" data-end="837">
<p data-start="795" data-end="837">Run shell commands: <code data-start="815" data-end="837">echo "Hello Jenkins"</code></p>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
<p data-start="839" data-end="860">✅ Confirm build logs.</p>

<h2 data-start="1148" data-end="1187">🧩 <strong data-start="1154" data-end="1187">3. Jenkins Pipelines (Groovy)</strong></h2>

      }

      }

      }
    }
  }
}

animation-duration: 1200ms;"><div class="cm-cursor cm-cursor-primary" style="left: 6px; top: 5.60059px; height: 18.3994px;"></div></div><div class="cm-layer cm-selectionLayer" aria-hidden="true" style="z-index: -2;"></div></div></div><p><code><span>Jenkinsfile</span></code><span>:</span></p><div class="cm-editor ͼ1 ͼ3 ͼ4 ͼ1o ͼ11j" data-is-code-block-view="true" contenteditable="false"><div class="cm-announced" aria-live="polite"></div><div tabindex="-1" class="cm-scroller"><div spellcheck="false" autocorrect="off" autocapitalize="off" translate="no" contenteditable="true" class="cm-content" role="textbox" aria-multiline="true" style="tab-size: 4;"><div class="cm-line">pipeline {</div><div class="cm-line">  agent any</div><div class="cm-line">  stages {</div><div class="cm-line">    stage('Docker Build') {</div><div class="cm-line">      steps {</div><div class="cm-line">        sh 'docker build -t myapp:latest .'</div><div class="cm-line">      }</div><div class="cm-line">    }</div><div class="cm-line">  }</div><div class="cm-line">}</div></div><div class="cm-layer cm-layer-above cm-cursorLayer" aria-hidden="true" style="z-index: 150; animation-duration: 1200ms;"><div class="cm-cursor cm-cursor-primary" style="left: 6px; top: 5.6001px; height: 18.3999px;"></div></div><div class="cm-layer cm-selectionLayer" aria-hidden="true" style="z-index: -2;"></div></div></div><div contenteditable="false"><hr></div><h3><span><strong>Lab 5: Parallel Execution Pipeline</strong></span></h3><p><span><strong>Jenkinsfile:</strong></span></p><div class="cm-editor ͼ1 ͼ3 ͼ4 ͼ1o ͼ11k" data-is-code-block-view="true" contenteditable="false"><div class="cm-announced" aria-live="polite"></div><div tabindex="-1" class="cm-scroller"><div spellcheck="false" autocorrect="off" autocapitalize="off" translate="no" contenteditable="true" class="cm-content" role="textbox" aria-multiline="true" style="tab-size: 4;"><div class="cm-line">pipeline {</div><div class="cm-line">  agent any</div><div class="cm-line">  stages {</div><div class="cm-line">    stage('Parallel Testing') {</div><div class="cm-line">      parallel {</div><div class="cm-line">        stage('Test A') {</div><div class="cm-line">          steps {</div><div class="cm-line">            echo 'Running Test A'</div><div class="cm-line">          }</div><div class="cm-line">        }</div><div class="cm-line">        stage('Test B') {</div><div class="cm-line">          steps {</div><div class="cm-line">            echo 'Running Test B'</div><div class="cm-line">          }</div><div class="cm-line">        }</div><div class="cm-line">      }</div><div class="cm-line">    }</div><div class="cm-line">  }</div><div class="cm-line">}</div></div><div class="cm-layer cm-layer-above cm-cursorLayer" aria-hidden="true" style="z-index: 150; animation-duration: 1200ms;"><div class="cm-cursor cm-cursor-primary" style="left: 6px; top: 5.6001px; height: 18.3999px;"></div></div><div class="cm-layer cm-selectionLayer" aria-hidden="true" style="z-index: -2;"></div></div></div><div contenteditable="false"><hr></div><h3><span><strong>Lab 6: Approval Step Pipeline</strong></span></h3><p><span><strong>Jenkinsfile:</strong></span></p><div class="cm-editor ͼ1 ͼ3 ͼ4 ͼ1o ͼ11l" data-is-code-block-view="true" contenteditable="false"><div class="cm-announced" aria-live="polite"></div><div tabindex="-1" class="cm-scroller"><div spellcheck="false" autocorrect="off" autocapitalize="off" translate="no" contenteditable="true" class="cm-content" role="textbox" aria-multiline="true" style="tab-size: 4;"><div class="cm-line">pipeline {</div><div class="cm-line">  agent any</div><div class="cm-line">  stages {</div><div class="cm-line">    stage('Approval') {</div><div class="cm-line">      steps {</div><div class="cm-line">        input 'Approve deployment?'</div><div class="cm-line">      }</div><div class="cm-line">    }</div><div class="cm-line">    stage('Deploy') {</div><div class="cm-line">      steps {</div><div class="cm-line">        echo 'Deployment started...'</div><div class="cm-line">      }</div><div class="cm-line">    }</div><div class="cm-line">  }</div><div class="cm-line">}</div></div><div class="cm-layer cm-layer-above cm-cursorLayer" aria-hidden="true" style="z-index: 150; Push') {</div><div class="cm-line">      steps {</div><div class="cm-line">        sh 'docker build -t my-node-app .'</div><div class="cm-line">      }</div><div class="cm-line">    }</div><div class="cm-line">  }</div><div class="cm-line">}</div></div><div class="cm-layer cm-layer-above cm-cursorLayer" aria-hidden="true" style="z-index: 150; <h2 data-start="155" data-end="201">🚀 <strong data-start="161" data-end="201">Lab 4: Jenkins Docker Build Pipeline</strong></h2>
<h3 data-start="203" data-end="228"><strong data-start="207" data-end="228">1. Prerequisites:</strong></h3>

language-groovy"><span>pipeline {
    agent any
    stages {
        stage('Checkout') {
            steps {
                git 'https://github.com/sample-repos/jenkins-docker-sample.git'
            }
        }
        stage('Docker Build') {
            steps {
                sh 'docker build -t my-python-app:latest .'
            }
        }
        stage('Docker Run') {
            steps {
                sh 'docker run --rm my-python-app:latest'
            }
        }
    }
}
</span></code></div></div></pre>

<h2 data-start="1719" data-end="1769">☸️ <strong data-start="1725" data-end="1769">Lab 10: Jenkins + Kubernetes Integration</strong></h2>
<h3 data-start="1771" data-end="1787"><strong data-start="1775" data-end="1787">1. Goal:</strong></h3>
<p data-start="1788" data-end="1862">Build app → push Docker image → deploy to Kubernetes via Jenkins Pipeline.</p>
<hr data-start="1864" data-end="1867">
<h3 data-start="1869" data-end="1899"><strong data-start="1873" data-end="1899">2. Kubernetes Cluster:</strong></h3>
<ul data-start="1900" data-end="2006">
<li data-start="1900" data-end="1954">
<p data-start="1902" data-end="1954">Local (e.g., Minikube/Kind/Kind-in-Docker) or cloud.</p>
</li>
<li data-start="1955" data-end="2006">
<p data-start="1957" data-end="2006"><code data-start="1957" data-end="1966">kubectl</code> installed &amp; configured on Jenkins node.</p>
</li>
</ul>
<hr data-start="2008" data-end="2011">

language-groovy"><span>pipeline {
    agent any
    environment {
        IMAGE = 'my-python-app:latest'
    }
    stages {
        stage('Checkout') {
            steps {
                git 'https://github.com/sample-repos/jenkins-docker-sample.git'
            }
        }
        stage('Docker Build &amp; Push') {
            steps {
                sh 'docker build -t $IMAGE .'
                // Example push (if DockerHub):
                // sh 'docker tag $IMAGE yourdockerhub/my-python-app:latest'
                // sh 'docker push yourdockerhub/my-python-app:latest'
            }
        }
        stage('Deploy to Kubernetes') {
            steps {
                sh 'kubectl apply -f k8s/deployment.yaml'
            }
        }
    }
}
</span></code></div></div></pre>

<h2 data-start="3615" data-end="3641">✅ <strong data-start="3620" data-end="3641">Next Suggestions:</strong></h2>

<li data-start="3642" data-end="3739">
<p data-start="3645" data-end="3739">Replace <strong data-start="3653" data-end="3668">local build</strong> with <strong data-start="3674" data-end="3713">DockerHub/GitHub Container Registry</strong> for real-world scenarios.</p>
</li>
<li data-start="3740" data-end="3802">
<p data-start="3743" data-end="3802">Add <strong data-start="3747" data-end="3762">Helm charts</strong> for more complex Kubernetes deployment.</p>
</li>
<li data-start="3803" data-end="3878">
<p data-start="3806" data-end="3878">Enable <strong data-start="3813" data-end="3853">dynamic Jenkins agents on Kubernetes</strong> (via Kubernetes plugin).</p>
</li>
</ol>

class="markdown prose dark:prose-invert w-full break-words light"><p data-start="0" data-end="140">Great choice.<br data-start="13" data-end="16">
Dynamic Jenkins agents (pods) in Kubernetes are the <strong data-start="68" data-end="139">modern, scalable way to run Jenkins builds without permanent agents</strong>.</p>
<p data-start="142" data-end="172">Let’s cover this step by step.</p>
<hr data-start="174" data-end="177">
<h2 data-start="179" data-end="233">☸️ <strong data-start="185" data-end="233">Lab 11: Jenkins Dynamic Agents on Kubernetes</strong></h2>
<hr data-start="235" data-end="238">
<h3 data-start="240" data-end="264"><strong data-start="244" data-end="264">1. Prerequisites</strong></h3>
<p data-start="265" data-end="430">✔️ Kubernetes Cluster running (Minikube/Kind/K8s cluster)<br data-start="322" data-end="325">
✔️ Helm installed (<code data-start="344" data-end="349">v3+</code>)<br data-start="350" data-end="353">
✔️ <code data-start="356" data-end="365">kubectl</code> working<br data-start="373" data-end="376">
✔️ Docker registry (optional for pushing build images)</p>
<hr data-start="432" data-end="435">
<h3 data-start="437" data-end="495"><strong data-start="441" data-end="495">2. Install Jenkins via Helm with Kubernetes Plugin</strong></h3>

<hr data-start="902" data-end="905">
<h3 data-start="907" data-end="981"><strong data-start="911" data-end="981">3. Install Kubernetes Plugin in Jenkins (Auto-installed via chart)</strong></h3>
<p data-start="983" data-end="1016">Already enabled if you used Helm.</p>
<p data-start="1018" data-end="1091">Check in Jenkins:<br data-start="1035" data-end="1038">
<strong data-start="1038" data-end="1091">Manage Jenkins &gt; Plugins &gt; Installed &gt; Kubernetes</strong></p>
<hr data-start="1093" data-end="1096">
<h3 data-start="1098" data-end="1147"><strong data-start="1102" data-end="1147">4. Configure Kubernetes Cloud in Jenkins:</strong></h3>
<p data-start="1149" data-end="1200"><strong data-start="1149" data-end="1199">Manage Jenkins &gt; Configure Clouds &gt; Kubernetes</strong>:</p>
<ul data-start="1202" data-end="1453">
<li data-start="1202" data-end="1250">
<p data-start="1204" data-end="1250"><strong data-start="1204" data-end="1223">Kubernetes URL:</strong> <a data-start="1224" data-end="1250" rel="noopener" target="_new" class="cursor-pointer">https://kubernetes.default</a></p>
</li>
<li data-start="1251" data-end="1324">
<p data-start="1253" data-end="1324"><strong data-start="1253" data-end="1278">Kubernetes Namespace:</strong> default (or the namespace Jenkins is running)</p>
</li>
<li data-start="1325" data-end="1388">
<p data-start="1327" data-end="1388"><strong data-start="1327" data-end="1343">Credentials:</strong> “Kubernetes service account” (auto-detected)</p>
</li>
<li data-start="1389" data-end="1453">
<p data-start="1391" data-end="1453"><strong data-start="1391" data-end="1407">Jenkins URL:</strong> <a data-start="1408" data-end="1453" rel="noopener" target="_new" class="cursor-pointer">http://jenkins.default.svc.cluster.local:8080</a></p>
</li>
</ul>
<hr data-start="1455" data-end="1458">
<h3 data-start="1460" data-end="1491"><strong data-start="1464" data-end="1491">5. Define Pod Template:</strong></h3>
<p data-start="1493" data-end="1528">In same page (or via Jenkinsfiles):</p>
<p data-start="1530" data-end="1588">✔️ Example: <strong data-start="1542" data-end="1566">Minimal Pod Template</strong> with Docker + kubectl</p>

<h3 data-start="1815" data-end="1857"><strong data-start="1819" data-end="1857">6. Jenkinsfile with Dynamic Agent:</strong></h3>
<pre class="overflow-visible!" data-start="1859" data-end="2417"><div class="contain-inline-size rounded-2xl border-[0.5px] border-token-border-medium relative bg-token-sidebar-surface-primary"><div stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"></path><path d="M5.66282 16.5231L5.18413 19.3952C5.12203 19.7678 5.09098 19.9541 5.14876 20.0888C5.19933 20.2067 5.29328 20.3007 5.41118 20.3512C5.54589 15.0458C5.85062 15.3963 5.78802 15.7719 5.66282 16.5231Z" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"></path><path d="M14.5 7L18.5 11" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"></path></svg>Edit</button></span></div></div></div><div class="overflow-y-auto p-4" dir="ltr"><code class="whitespace-pre! language-groovy"><span>pipeline {
  agent {
    kubernetes {
      yaml """
apiVersion: v1
kind: Pod
spec:
  containers:
  - name: docker
    image: docker:24
    command:
    - cat
    tty: true
  - name: kubectl
    image: bitnami/kubectl:latest
    command:
    - cat
    tty: true
"""
    }
  }
  stages {
    stage('Build') {
      steps {
        container('docker') {
          sh 'docker --version'
        }
      }
    }
    stage('Deploy') {
      steps {
        container('kubectl') {
          sh 'kubectl version --client'
        }
      }
    }
  }
}
</span></code></div></div></pre>
<p data-start="2419" data-end="2497">✔️ <strong data-start="2422" data-end="2477">Jenkins will spawn a pod for this build dynamically</strong> — no static agents!</p>
<hr data-start="2499" data-end="2502">

<p data-start="2565" data-end="2642">You’ll see Jenkins agent pods spun up and terminated automatically per build.</p>
<hr data-start="2644" data-end="2647">
<h3 data-start="2649" data-end="2702"><strong data-start="2653" data-end="2702">8. (Optional) Push Docker Images to Registry:</strong></h3>
<ul data-start="2704" data-end="2821">
<li data-start="2704" data-end="2736">
<p data-start="2706" data-end="2736">Mount Docker config as secret.</p>
</li>
<li data-start="2737" data-end="2821">
<p data-start="2739" data-end="2821">Use <code data-start="2743" data-end="2751">kaniko</code> or <code data-start="2755" data-end="2764">buildah</code> to build images inside pods — no Docker daemon required.</p>
</li>
</ul>

✅ Agents dynamically spin up as Kubernetes pods<br data-start="2932" data-end="2935">
✅ Fully scalable &amp; efficient CI/CD setup</p>

class="react-scroll-to-bottom--css-hbsfs-79elbk h-full"><div class="react-scroll-to-bottom--css-hbsfs-1n7m0yu flex flex-col"><div class="block h-auto"><div class="h-full w-full"><div class="flex bg-transparent ProseMirror" contenteditable="false" style="width: 775px;" translate="no"><h1><span>Jenkins Dynamic Agents on Kubernetes - Hands-On Lab</span></h1><h2><span>1. Prerequisites</span></h2><ul data-spread="false"><li><p><span>Kubernetes Cluster (Minikube/Kind/Cloud K8s)</span></p></li><li><p><span>Helm v3+</span></p></li><li><p><span>kubectl configured</span></p></li><li><p><span>Docker registry (optional for image push)</span></p></li></ul><div contenteditable="false"><hr></div><h2><span>2. Install Jenkins via Helm</span></h2><div class="cm-editor ͼ1 ͼ3 ͼ4 ͼ1o ͼ11q" data-is-code-block-view="true" contenteditable="false"><div class="cm-announced" aria-live="polite"></div><div tabindex="-1" class="cm-scroller"><div spellcheck="false" autocorrect="off" autocapitalize="off" translate="no" contenteditable="true" class="cm-content" role="textbox" aria-multiline="true" data-language="shell" style="tab-size: 4;"><div class="cm-line">helm repo add jenkins https://charts.jenkins.io</div><div class="cm-line">helm repo update</div><div class="cm-line"><br></div><div class="cm-line">helm upgrade <span class="ͼ1r">--install</span> jenkins jenkins/jenkins \</div><div class="cm-line">  <span class="ͼ1r">--set</span> controller<span class="ͼ1r ͼg">.adminUser</span><span class="ͼ1w">=</span>admin \</div><div class="cm-line">  <span class="ͼ1r">--set</span> controller<span class="ͼ1r ͼg">.adminPassword</span><span class="ͼ1w">=</span>admin \</div><div class="cm-line">  <span class="ͼ1r">--set</span> controller<span class="ͼ1r ͼg">.serviceType</span><span class="ͼ1w">=</span>NodePort \</div><div class="cm-line">  <span class="ͼ1r">--set</span> controller.resources.requests<span class="ͼ1r ͼg">.cpu</span><span class="ͼ1w">=</span>500m \</div><div class="cm-line">  <span class="ͼ1r">--set</span> controller.resources.requests<span class="ͼ1r ͼg">.memory</span><span class="ͼ1w">=</span>512Mi</div></div><div class="cm-layer cm-layer-above cm-cursorLayer" aria-hidden="true" style="z-index: 150; animation-duration: 1200ms;"><div class="cm-cursor cm-cursor-primary" style="left: 6px; top: 5.59998px; height: 18.4px;"></div></div><div class="cm-layer cm-selectionLayer" aria-hidden="true" style="z-index: -2;"></div></div></div><p><span>Get Jenkins URL:</span></p><div class="cm-editor ͼ1 ͼ3 ͼ4 ͼ1o ͼ11r" data-is-code-block-view="true" contenteditable="false"><div class="cm-announced" aria-live="polite"></div><div tabindex="-1" class="cm-scroller"><div spellcheck="false" autocorrect="off" autocapitalize="off" translate="no" contenteditable="true" class="cm-content" role="textbox" aria-multiline="true" data-language="shell" style="tab-size: 4;"><div class="cm-line">kubectl <span class="ͼ1r">get</span> svc jenkins</div></div><div class="cm-layer cm-layer-above cm-cursorLayer" aria-hidden="true" style="z-index: 150; animation-duration: 1200ms;"><div class="cm-cursor cm-cursor-primary" style="left: 6px; top: 5.6001px; height: 18.3999px;"></div></div><div class="cm-layer cm-selectionLayer" aria-hidden="true" style="z-index: -2;"></div></div></div><div contenteditable="false"><hr></div><h2><span>3. Verify Kubernetes Plugin</span></h2><p><span>In Jenkins:</span></p><div class="cm-editor ͼ1 ͼ3 ͼ4 ͼ1o ͼ11s" data-is-code-block-view="true" contenteditable="false"><div class="cm-announced" aria-live="polite"></div><div tabindex="-1" class="cm-scroller"><div spellcheck="false" autocorrect="off" autocapitalize="off" translate="no" contenteditable="true" class="cm-content" role="textbox" aria-multiline="true" style="tab-size: 4;"><div class="cm-line">Manage Jenkins &gt; Plugins &gt; Installed &gt; Kubernetes</div></div><div class="cm-layer cm-layer-above cm-cursorLayer" aria-hidden="true" style="z-index: 150; animation-duration: 1200ms;"><div class="cm-cursor cm-cursor-primary" style="left: 6px; top: 5.6001px; height: 18.3999px;"></div></div><div class="cm-layer cm-selectionLayer" aria-hidden="true" style="z-index: -2;"></div></div></div><div contenteditable="false"><hr></div><h2><span>4. Configure Kubernetes Cloud in Jenkins</span></h2><div class="cm-editor ͼ1 ͼ3 ͼ4 ͼ1o ͼ11t" data-is-code-block-view="true" contenteditable="false"><div class="cm-announced" aria-live="polite"></div><div tabindex="-1" class="cm-scroller"><div spellcheck="false" autocorrect="off" autocapitalize="off" translate="no" contenteditable="true" class="cm-content" role="textbox" aria-multiline="true" style="tab-size: 4;"><div class="cm-line">Manage Jenkins &gt; Configure Clouds &gt; Kubernetes</div></div><div class="cm-layer cm-layer-above cm-cursorLayer" aria-hidden="true" style="z-index: 150; animation-duration: 1200ms;"><div class="cm-cursor cm-cursor-primary" style="left: 6px; top: 5.59985px; height: 18.4001px;"></div></div><div class="cm-layer cm-selectionLayer" aria-hidden="true" style="z-index: -2;"></div></div></div><ul data-spread="false"><li><p><span>Kubernetes URL: </span><code><span>https://kubernetes.default</span></code></p></li><li><p><span>Namespace: </span><code><span>default</span></code></p></li><li><p><span>Credentials: "Kubernetes service account" (auto-detected)</span></p></li><li><p><span>Jenkins URL: </span><code><span>http://jenkins.default.svc.cluster.local:8080</span></code></p></li></ul><div contenteditable="false"><hr></div><h2><span>5. Define Pod Template</span></h2><p><span>Example Pod Template:</span></p><div class="cm-editor ͼ1 ͼ3 ͼ4 ͼ1o ͼ11u" data-is-code-block-view="true" contenteditable="false"><div class="cm-announced" aria-live="polite"></div><div tabindex="-1" class="cm-scroller"><div spellcheck="false" autocorrect="off" autocapitalize="off" translate="no" contenteditable="true" class="cm-content" role="textbox" aria-multiline="true" data-language="yaml" style="tab-size: 4;"><div class="cm-line"><span class="ͼ1r ͼl">containers</span><span class="ͼ1w">:</span></div><div class="cm-line"><span class="ͼ1w">-</span> <span class="ͼ1r ͼl">name</span><span class="ͼ1w">:</span> jnlp</div><div class="cm-line">  <span class="ͼ1r ͼl">image</span><span class="ͼ1w">:</span> jenkins/inbound-agent:latest</div><div class="cm-line"><span class="ͼ1w">-</span> <span class="ͼ1r ͼl">name</span><span class="ͼ1w">:</span> docker</div><div class="cm-line">  <span class="ͼ1r ͼl">image</span><span class="ͼ1w">:</span> docker:24</div><div class="cm-line">  <span class="ͼ1r ͼl">command</span><span class="ͼ1w">:</span></div><div class="cm-line">  <span class="ͼ1w">-</span> cat</div><div class="cm-line">  <span class="ͼ1r ͼl">tty</span><span class="ͼ1w">:</span> true</div><div class="cm-line"><span class="ͼ1w">-</span> <span class="ͼ1r ͼl">name</span><span class="ͼ1w">:</span> kubectl</div><div class="cm-line">  <span class="ͼ1r ͼl">image</span><span class="ͼ1w">:</span> bitnami/kubectl:latest</div><div class="cm-line">  <span class="ͼ1r ͼl">command</span><span class="ͼ1w">:</span></div><div class="cm-line">  <span class="ͼ1w">-</span> cat</div><div class="cm-line">  <span class="ͼ1r ͼl">tty</span><span class="ͼ1w">:</span> true</div></div><div class="cm-layer cm-layer-above cm-cursorLayer" aria-hidden="true" style="z-index: 150; animation-duration: 1200ms;"><div class="cm-cursor cm-cursor-primary" style="left: 6px; top: 5.6001px; height: 18.3999px;"></div></div><div class="cm-layer cm-selectionLayer" aria-hidden="true" style="z-index: -2;"></div></div></div><div contenteditable="false"><hr></div><h2><span>6. Jenkinsfile Example</span></h2><div class="cm-editor ͼ1 ͼ3 ͼ4 ͼ1o ͼ11v" data-is-code-block-view="true" contenteditable="false"><div class="cm-announced" aria-live="polite"></div><div tabindex="-1" class="cm-scroller"><div spellcheck="false" autocorrect="off" autocapitalize="off" translate="no" contenteditable="true" class="cm-content" role="textbox" aria-multiline="true" style="tab-size: 4;"><div class="cm-line">pipeline {</div><div class="cm-line">  agent {</div><div class="cm-line">    kubernetes {</div><div class="cm-line">      yaml """</div><div class="cm-line">apiVersion: v1</div><div class="cm-line">kind: Pod</div><div class="cm-line">spec:</div><div class="cm-line">  containers:</div><div class="cm-line">  - name: docker</div><div class="cm-line">    image: docker:24</div><div class="cm-line">    command:</div><div class="cm-line">    - cat</div><div class="cm-line">    tty: true</div><div class="cm-line">  - name: kubectl</div><div class="cm-line">    image: bitnami/kubectl:latest</div><div class="cm-line">    command:</div><div class="cm-line">    - cat</div><div class="cm-line">    tty: true</div><div class="cm-line">"""</div><div class="cm-line">    }</div><div class="cm-line">  }</div><div class="cm-line">  stages {</div><div class="cm-line">    stage('Build') {</div><div class="cm-line">      steps {</div><div class="cm-line">        container('docker') {</div><div class="cm-line">          sh 'docker --version'</div><div class="cm-line">        }</div><div class="cm-line">      }</div><div class="cm-line">    }</div><div class="cm-line">    stage('Deploy') {</div><div class="cm-line">      steps {</div><div class="cm-line">        container('kubectl') {</div><div class="cm-line">          sh 'kubectl version --client'</div><div class="cm-line">        }</div><div class="cm-line">      }</div><div class="cm-line">    }</div><div class="cm-gap" style="height: 28px;"></div></div><div class="cm-layer cm-layer-above cm-cursorLayer" aria-hidden="true" style="z-index: 150; animation-duration: 1200ms;"><div class="cm-cursor cm-cursor-primary" style="left: 6px; top: 5.6001px; height: 18.3999px;"></div></div><div class="cm-layer cm-selectionLayer" aria-hidden="true" style="z-index: -2;"></div></div></div><div contenteditable="false"><hr></div><h2><span>7. <h2 data-start="53" data-end="109">🔥 <strong data-start="59" data-end="107">Jenkins Helm-Based Kubernetes Deployment Lab</strong></h2>
<h3 data-start="111" data-end="126"><strong data-start="115" data-end="124">Goal:</strong></h3>
<p data-start="127" data-end="275">Build a Docker image in Jenkins, push it to a container registry, and deploy the app to Kubernetes using Helm (all automated in a Jenkins pipeline).</p>
<hr data-start="277" data-end="280">
<h2 data-start="282" data-end="307"><strong data-start="285" data-end="305">1. Prerequisites</strong></h2>
<p data-start="309" data-end="520">✔️ Previous Dynamic Agent setup (from your last lab)<br data-start="361" data-end="364">
✔️ Kubernetes Cluster ready<br data-start="391" data-end="394">
✔️ Helm v3+ installed<br data-start="415" data-end="418">
✔️ Docker Registry (Docker Hub / Harbor / ECR / etc.)<br data-start="471" data-end="474">
✔️ Simple app with a Dockerfile and Helm chart</p>
<hr data-start="522" data-end="525">

<pre class="overflow-visible!" data-start="1341" data-end="2717"><div class="contain-inline-size rounded-2xl border-[0.5px] border-token-border-medium relative bg-token-sidebar-surface-primary"><div 15.6569 20.6569 17 19 17H17V19C17 20.6569 15.6569 22 14 22H5C3.34315 22 2 20.6569 2 19V10C2 8.34315 3.34315 7 5 7H7V5ZM9 7H14C15.6569 7 17 8.34315 17 10V15H19C19.5523 15 20 14.5523 20 14V5C20 4.44772 fill="currentColor"></path></svg>Copy</button><span class="" data-state="closed"><button class="flex items-center gap-1 py-1 select-none"><svg width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" class="icon-xs"><path d="M2.5 5.5C4.3 5.2 5.2 4 5.5 2.5C5.8 4 6.7 5.2 8.5 5.5C6.7 5.8 5.8 7 5.5 8.5C5.2 7 4.3 5.8 2.5 5.5Z" fill="currentColor" stroke="currentColor" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"></path><path d="M5.66282 16.5231L5.18413 19.3952C5.12203 19.7678 5.09098 19.9541 5.14876 20.0888C5.19933 20.2067 5.29328 20.3007 5.41118 20.3512C5.54589 20.409 5.73218 20.378 6.10476 20.3159L8.97693 19.8372C9.72813 19.712 10.1037 19.6494 10.4542 19.521C10.7652 19.407 11.0608 19.2549 11.3343 19.068C11.6425 18.8575 11.9118 18.5882 12.4503 18.0497L20 10.5C21.3807 9.11929 21.3807 6.88071 20 5.5C18.6193 4.11929 16.3807 4.11929 15 5.5L7.45026 13.0497C6.91175 13.5882 6.6425 13.8575 6.43197 14.1657C6.24513 14.4392 6.09299 14.7348 5.97903 15.0458C5.85062 15.3963 5.78802 15.7719 5.66282 16.5231Z" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"></path><path d="M14.5 7L18.5 11" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"></path></svg>Edit</button></span></div></div></div><div class="overflow-y-auto p-4" dir="ltr"><code class="whitespace-pre! language-groovy"><span>pipeline {
    agent {
        kubernetes {
            yaml '''
apiVersion: v1
kind: Pod
spec:
  containers:
  - name: docker
    image: docker:24
    command: ["cat"]
    tty: true
  - name: helm
    image: alpine/helm:3.14.0
    command: ["cat"]
    tty: true
'''
        }
    }
    environment {
        REGISTRY = 'docker.io'
        IMAGE_NAME = 'your-docker-username/my-app'
    }
    stages {
        stage('Build Image') {
            steps {
                container('docker') {
                    sh 'docker build -t $REGISTRY/$IMAGE_NAME:latest .'
                }
            }
        }
        stage('Push Image') {
            steps {
                container('docker') {
                    withCredentials([usernamePassword(credentialsId: 'dockerhub-creds', usernameVariable: 'DOCKER_USER', passwordVariable: 'DOCKER_PASS')]) {
                        sh 'echo $DOCKER_PASS | docker login -u $DOCKER_USER --password-stdin $REGISTRY'
                        sh 'docker push $REGISTRY/$IMAGE_NAME:latest'
                    }
                }
            }
        }
        stage('Deploy with Helm') {
            steps {
                container('helm') {
                    sh 'helm upgrade --install my-app ./chart --set image.repository=$REGISTRY/$IMAGE_NAME --set image.tag=latest'
                }
            }
        }
    }
}
</span></code></div></div></pre>
<hr data-start="2719" data-end="2722">

<p data-start="2766" data-end="2787">ID: <code data-start="2770" data-end="2787">dockerhub-creds</code></p>
</li>
<li data-start="2788" data-end="2817">
<p data-start="2790" data-end="2817">Type: <strong data-start="2796" data-end="2817">Username/Password</strong></p>
</li>

<p data-start="2820" data-end="2857">DockerHub username and password/token</p>
</li>
</ul>

<h2 data-start="3096" data-end="3198">✅ <strong data-start="3101" data-end="3198">Next Possible Lab: Kaniko Dockerless Image Build in Jenkins + Helm Deploy (fully Docker-free)</strong></h2>

<p data-start="3205" data-end="3333" data-is-last-node="" data-is-only-node="">Would you like me to save this Helm lab as a <strong data-start="3250" data-end="3280">Markdown file for download</strong> or proceed to the <strong data-start="3299" data-end="3332">Kaniko Dockerless Jenkins lab</strong>?</p></div></div></div></div><div class="flex min-h-[46px] justify-start"><div
